   185 
   186 interface LanguageContextType {
   187   language: Language;
   188   setLanguage: (lang: Language) => void;
   189   t: (path: string) => string;
   190 }
   191 
   192 const LanguageContext = createContext<LanguageContextType | undefined>(undefined);
   193 
   194 export const LanguageProvider: React.FC<{ children: React.ReactNode }> = ({ children }) => {
   195   const [language, setLanguage] = useState<Language>(() => {
   196     return (localStorage.getItem('language') as Language) || 'zh-CN';
   197   });
   198 
   199   useEffect(() => {
   200     localStorage.setItem('language', language);
   201   }, [language]);
   202 
   203   const t = (path: string): string => {
   204     const keys = path.split('.');
   205     let current: any = translations[language];
   206     for (const key of keys) {
   207       if (current[key] === undefined) return path;
   208       current = current[key];
   209     }
   210     return current;
   211   };
   212 
   213   return (
   214     <LanguageContext.Provider value={{ language, setLanguage, t }}>
   215       {children}
   216     </LanguageContext.Provider>
   217   );
   218 };
   219 
   220 export const useLanguage = () => {
   221   const context = useContext(LanguageContext);
   222   if (!context) throw new Error('useLanguage must be used within LanguageProvider');
   223   return context;
   224 };
   225 
   226 // Theme Context
   227 type Theme = 'light' | 'dark' | 'system';
   228 
   229 interface ThemeContextType {
   230   theme: Theme;
   231   setTheme: (theme: Theme) => void;
   232   actualTheme: 'light' | 'dark';
   233 }
   234 
   235 const ThemeContext = createContext<ThemeContextType | undefined>(undefined);
   236 
   237 export const ThemeProvider: React.FC<{ children: React.ReactNode }> = ({ children }) => {
   238   const [theme, setTheme] = useState<Theme>(() => {
   239     return (localStorage.getItem('theme') as Theme) || 'system';
   240   });
   241 
   242   const [actualTheme, setActualTheme] = useState<'light' | 'dark'>('light');
   243 
   244   useEffect(() => {
   245     localStorage.setItem('theme', theme);
   246     const root = window.document.documentElement;
   247     
   248     const applyTheme = (t: 'light' | 'dark') => {
   249       root.classList.remove('light', 'dark');
   250       root.classList.add(t);
   251       setActualTheme(t);
   252     };
   253 
   254     if (theme === 'system') {
   255       const systemTheme = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches ? 'dark' : 'light';
   256       applyTheme(systemTheme);
   257       
   258       const mediaQuery = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
   259       const handleChange = (e: MediaQueryListEvent) => {
   260         applyTheme(e.matches ? 'dark' : 'light');
   261       };
   262       mediaQuery.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
   263       return () => mediaQuery.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
   264     } else {
   265       applyTheme(theme);
   266     }
   267   }, [theme]);
   268 
   269   return (
   270     <ThemeContext.Provider value={{ theme, setTheme, actualTheme }}>
   271       {children}
   272     </ThemeContext.Provider>
   273   );
   274 };
   275 
   276 export const useTheme = () => {
   277   const context = useContext(ThemeContext);
   278   if (!context) throw new Error('useTheme must be used within ThemeProvider');
   279   return context;
   280 };

Here's the result of running `cat -n` on the file: /workspace/app-bbkfg9ldx9mp/src/components/SkillsSection.tsx:
     1 import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
     2 import { BASE_DATE, BASE_DURATION, SKILLS } from "@/lib/data";
     3 import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge";
     4 import { useLanguage } from "@/contexts/AppContext";
     5 
     6 export function SkillsSection() {
     7   const [duration, setDuration] = useState(BASE_DURATION);
     8   const { t, language } = useLanguage();
     9 
    10   useEffect(() => {
    11     const timer = setInterval(() => {
    12       const now = new Date();
    13       const diffMs = now.getTime() - BASE_DATE.getTime();
    14       const diffDays = Math.floor(diffMs / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
    15       
    16       let years = BASE_DURATION.years;
    17       let months = BASE_DURATION.months;
    18       let days = BASE_DURATION.days + diffDays;
    19 
    20       while (days >= 30) {
    21         days -= 30;
    22         months += 1;
    23       }
    24       while (months >= 12) {
    25         months -= 12;
    26         years += 1;
    27       }
    28 
    29       setDuration({ years, months, days });
    30     }, 1000);
    31 
    32     return () => clearInterval(timer);
    33   }, []);
    34 
    35   const getCategoryLabel = (cat: string) => {
    36     const map: Record<string, string> = {
    37       "前端开发": "frontend",
    38       "后端开发": "backend",
    39       "客户端 & 其他": "client",
    40       "数据库": "db",
    41       "运维工具": "ops",
    42       "运行环境": "env",
    43       "开发工具": "tools"
    44     };
    45     const key = map[cat];
    46     return key ? t(`skills.${key}`) : cat;
    47   };
    48 
    49   const unitMap: Record<string, {y: string, m: string, d: string}> = {
    50     'zh-CN': { y: '年', m: '月', d: '天' },
    51     'zh-TW': { y: '年', m: '月', d: '天' },
    52     'en': { y: ' Years', m: ' Months', d: ' Days' }
    53   };
    54   const units = unitMap[language];
    55 
    56   return (
    57     <div className="space-y-6">
    58       <div className="paper-card hand-border bg-muted/30">
    59         <h2 className="text-2xl mb-2">{t('skills.duration')}</h2>
    60         <div className="text-3xl font-hand-semibold animate-pulse">
    61           {duration.years}{units.y} {duration.months}{units.m} {duration.days}{units.d}
    62         </div>
    63         <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-2">({t('skills.duration')} - AUTO)</p>
    64       </div>
    65 
    66       <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
    67         {SKILLS.map((skill, idx) => (
    68           <div key={idx} className="paper-card hand-border">
    69             <h3 className="text-xl mb-3 border-b border-primary/20 pb-1">
    70               {getCategoryLabel(skill.category)}
    71             </h3>
    72             <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
    73               {skill.items.map((item, i) => (
    74                 <Badge key={i} variant="outline" className="border-primary/40 hover:bg-primary hover:text-white transition-colors">
    75                   {item}
    76                 </Badge>
    77               ))}
    78             </div>
    79           </div>
    80         ))}
    81       </div>
    82     </div>
    83   );
    84 }
    85

import { PROJECTS } from "@/lib/data";
import { Github, ExternalLink } from "lucide-react";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { useLanguage } from "@/contexts/AppContext";

export function ProjectList() {
  const { t } = useLanguage();
  const projectItems: any = t('projects.items');

  const getProjectDesc = (name: string, fallback: string) => {
    const keyMap: Record<string, string> = {
      "LangBot": "langbot",
      "Xmail Pro": "xmail",
      "Campux": "campux",
      "在线C++IDE": "cpp_ide",
      "云端图片储存平台": "img_cloud",
      "AI智能助手": "ai_assistant",
      "Hydro-OJ-IDE": "hydro_oj",
      "Free-one-api": "free_one_api",
      "个人主页": "personal_home"
    };
    const key = keyMap[name];
    return projectItems[key] || fallback;
  };

  return (
    <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
      {PROJECTS.map((project, idx) => (
        <div key={idx} className="paper-card hand-border flex flex-col h-full group hover:-translate-y-1 transition-transform">
          <div className="flex-1">
            <h3 className="text-2xl mb-2 group-hover:underline underline-offset-4 decoration-primary/50">
              {project.name}
            </h3>
            <p className="text-muted-foreground leading-relaxed">
              {getProjectDesc(project.name, project.desc)}
            </p>
          </div>
          <div className="mt-4 flex gap-2">
            {project.github && (
              <Button variant="outline" size="sm" asChild className="hand-border flex-1">
                <a href={project.github} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">
                  <Github className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" /> {t('projects.github')}
                </a>
              </Button>
            )}
            {project.site && (
              <Button variant="outline" size="sm" asChild className="hand-border flex-1">
                <a href={project.site} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">
                  <ExternalLink className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" /> {t('projects.site')}
                </a>
              </Button>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}

    27 export default function ContactPage() {
    28   const { t } = useLanguage();
    29   const [copiedIdx, setCopiedIdx] = useState<number | null>(null);
    30 
    31   const handleCopy = (text: string, idx: number) => {
    32     navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);
    33     setCopiedIdx(idx);

    35     setTimeout(() => setCopiedIdx(null), 2000);
    36   };
    37

     1 import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
     2 import { BASE_DATE, BASE_DURATION, SKILLS } from "@/lib/data";
     3 import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge";
     4 import { useLanguage } from "@/contexts/AppContext";
     5 
     6 export function SkillsSection() {
     7   const [duration, setDuration] = useState(BASE_DURATION);
     8   const { t, language } = useLanguage();
     9 
    10   useEffect(() => {
    11     const timer = setInterval(() => {
    12       const now = new Date();
    13       const diffMs = now.getTime() - BASE_DATE.getTime();
    14       const diffDays = Math.floor(diffMs / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
    15       
    16       let years = BASE_DURATION.years;
    17       let months = BASE_DURATION.months;
    18       let days = BASE_DURATION.days + diffDays;
    19 
    20       while (days >= 30) {
    21         days -= 30;
    22         months += 1;
    23       }
    24       while (months >= 12) {
    25         months -= 12;
    26         years += 1;
    27       }
    28 
    29       setDuration({ years, months, days });
    30     }, 1000);
    31 
    32     return () => clearInterval(timer);
    33   }, []);
    34 
    35   const getCategoryLabel = (cat: string) => {
    36     const map: Record<string, string> = {
    37       "前端开发": "frontend",
    38       "后端开发": "backend",
    39       "客户端 & 其他": "client",
    40       "数据库": "db",
    41       "运维工具": "ops",
    42       "运行环境": "env",
    43       "开发工具": "tools"
    44     };
    45     const key = map[cat];
    46     return key ? t(`skills.${key}`) : cat;
    47   };
    48 
    49   const unitMap: Record<string, {y: string, m: string, d: string}> = {
    50     'zh-CN': { y: '年', m: '月', d: '天' },
    51     'zh-TW': { y: '年', m: '月', d: '天' },
    52     'en': { y: ' Years', m: ' Months', d: ' Days' }
    53   };
    54   const units = unitMap[language];
    55 
    56   return (
    57     <div className="space-y-6">
    58       <div className="paper-card hand-border bg-muted/30">
    59         <h2 className="text-2xl mb-2">{t('skills.duration')}</h2>
    60         <div className="text-3xl font-hand-semibold animate-pulse">
    61           {duration.years}{units.y} {duration.months}{units.m} {duration.days}{units.d}
    62         </div>
    63         <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-2">({t('skills.duration')} - AUTO)</p>
    64       </div>
    65 
    66       <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
    67         {SKILLS.map((skill, idx) => (
    68           <div key={idx} className="paper-card hand-border">
    69             <h3 className="text-xl mb-3 border-b border-primary/20 pb-1">
    70               {getCategoryLabel(skill.category)}
    71             </h3>
    72             <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
    73               {skill.items.map((item, i) => (
    74                 <Badge key={i} variant="outline" className="border-primary/40 hover:bg-primary hover:text-white transition-colors">
    75                   {item}
    76                 </Badge>
    77               ))}
    78             </div>
    79           </div>
    80         ))}
    81       </div>
    82     </div>
    83   );

import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { BASE_DATE, BASE_DURATION, SKILLS } from "@/lib/data";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge";
import { useLanguage } from "@/contexts/AppContext";
import { 
  Code2, 
  Terminal, 
  Database, 
  Settings, 
  Monitor, 
  Wrench, 
  Layers,
  Clock
} from "lucide-react";

const categoryIconMap: Record<string, any> = {
  "frontend": Code2,
  "backend": Terminal,
  "client": Layers,
  "db": Database,
  "ops": Settings,
  "env": Monitor,
  "tools": Wrench
};

export function SkillsSection() {
  const [duration, setDuration] = useState(BASE_DURATION);
  const { t, language } = useLanguage();

  useEffect(() => {
    const timer = setInterval(() => {
      const now = new Date();
      const diffMs = now.getTime() - BASE_DATE.getTime();
      const diffDays = Math.floor(diffMs / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
      
      let years = BASE_DURATION.years;
      let months = BASE_DURATION.months;
      let days = BASE_DURATION.days + diffDays;

      while (days >= 30) {
        days -= 30;
        months += 1;
      }
      while (months >= 12) {
        months -= 12;
        years += 1;
      }

      setDuration({ years, months, days });
    }, 1000);

    return () => clearInterval(timer);
  }, []);

  const getCategoryInfo = (cat: string) => {
    const map: Record<string, string> = {
      "前端开发": "frontend",
      "后端开发": "backend",
      "客户端 & 其他": "client",
      "数据库": "db",
      "运维工具": "ops",
      "运行环境": "env",
      "开发工具": "tools"
    };
    const key = map[cat] || "tools";
    return {
      key,
      label: t(`skills.${key}`),
      Icon: categoryIconMap[key] || Wrench
    };
  };

  const unitMap: Record<string, {y: string, m: string, d: string}> = {
    'zh-CN': { y: '年', m: '月', d: '天' },
    'zh-TW': { y: '年', m: '月', d: '天' },
    'en': { y: ' Years', m: ' Months', d: ' Days' }
  };
  const units = unitMap[language] || unitMap['en'];

  return (
    <div className="space-y-12">
      <div className="paper-3d-black p-8 text-center space-y-4">
        <div className="flex justify-center">
          <Clock className="w-12 h-12 animate-spin-slow" />
        </div>
        <h2 className="text-3xl">{t('skills.duration')}</h2>
        <div className="text-4xl md:text-5xl font-hand-semibold tracking-wider">
          {duration.years}{units.y} {duration.months}{units.m} {duration.days}{units.d}
        </div>
        <p className="opacity-60 italic text-sm">Keep Learning, Keep Growing</p>
      </div>

      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-8">
        {SKILLS.map((skill, idx) => {
          const { label, Icon } = getCategoryInfo(skill.category);
          return (
            <div key={idx} className="paper-3d-white p-6 space-y-4 group hover:-translate-y-2 transition-all">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-lg bg-primary/5 flex items-center justify-center text-primary group-hover:bg-primary group-hover:text-primary-foreground transition-colors">
                  <Icon size={20} />
                </div>
                <h3 className="text-2xl">{label}</h3>
              </div>
              <div className="hand-divider opacity-10 !my-2" />
              <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                {skill.items.map((item, i) => {
                  const itemMap: Record<string, string> = {
                    "宝塔面板": "bt_panel",

                    "客户端 & 其他": "client_other"

                    </Badge>
                  );
                })}
              </div>
            </div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

    const key = keyMap[name];
    return projectItems[key] || fallback;
  };

  return (
    <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
      {PROJECTS.map((project, idx) => (
        <div key={idx} className="paper-card hand-border flex flex-col h-full group hover:-translate-y-1 transition-transform">
          <div className="flex-1">
            <h3 className="text-2xl mb-2 group-hover:underline underline-offset-4 decoration-primary/50">
              {project.name}
            </h3>
            <p className="text-muted-foreground leading-relaxed">
              {getProjectDesc(project.name, project.desc)}
            </p>
          </div>
          <div className="mt-4 flex gap-2">
            {project.github && (
              <Button variant="outline" size="sm" asChild className="hand-border flex-1">
                <a href={project.github} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">
                  <Github className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" /> {t('projects.github')}
                </a>
              </Button>
            )}
            {project.site && (
              <Button variant="outline" size="sm" asChild className="hand-border flex-1">
                <a href={project.site} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">
                  <ExternalLink className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" /> {t('projects.site')}
                </a>
              </Button>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}

import { PROJECTS } from "@/lib/data";
import { Github, ExternalLink, Hash } from "lucide-react";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { useLanguage } from "@/contexts/AppContext";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge";

export function ProjectList() {
  const { t } = useLanguage();
  const projectItems: any = t('projects.items');

  const getProjectDesc = (name: string, fallback: string) => {
    const keyMap: Record<string, string> = {
      "LangBot": "langbot",
      "Xmail Pro": "xmail",
      "Campux": "campux",
      "在线C++IDE": "cpp_ide",
      "云端图片储存平台": "img_cloud",
      "AI智能助手": "ai_assistant",
      "Hydro-OJ-IDE": "hydro_oj",
      "Free-one-api": "free_one_api",
      "个人主页": "personal_home"
    };
    const key = keyMap[name];
    return projectItems[key] || fallback;
  };

  return (
    <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-10">
      {PROJECTS.map((project, idx) => (
        <div key={idx} className="paper-3d-white flex flex-col h-full group overflow-hidden">
          <div className="p-8 flex-1 space-y-6">
            <div className="flex items-start justify-between">
              <h3 className="text-3xl font-hand-semibold group-hover:text-primary transition-colors">
                {project.name}
              </h3>
              <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-primary/5 flex items-center justify-center opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity">
                <Hash size={20} />
              </div>
            </div>
            
            <p className="text-muted-foreground leading-relaxed text-lg min-h-[80px]">
              {getProjectDesc(project.name, project.desc)}
            </p>

            <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 pt-2">
              {project.tags?.map((tag, i) => (
                <Badge key={i} variant="outline" className="hand-border bg-background/50 border-primary/20 text-xs py-0 h-6">
                  {tag}
                </Badge>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>

          <div className="p-6 bg-muted/20 border-t-2 border-primary/10 flex gap-4">
            {project.github && (
              <Button variant="outline" size="sm" asChild className="hand-border flex-1 h-11 bg-background hover:bg-primary hover:text-primary-foreground transition-all">
                <a href={project.github} target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">
                  <Github className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" /> {t('projects.github')}

                  <ExternalLink className="mr-2 h-4 w-4" /> {t('projects.site')}
                </a>
              </Button>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}
